 mohammad rafee kaa janm 24 disambar 1924 ko punjab ke kotla sultan singh gaanv main hua or 31 july 1980 ko unka nidhan ho gaya
 On the death anniversary of this great personality, let us know 10 special things about him
 1
 There is very little kind man like Mohammed Rafi, he never used to ask the composer how much money he would get for singing a song
 vah sirf aakar geet ga diya karte the or kabhi-kabhi to 1 rupee ko lekar bhi geet unhone gaaya he
 2
 suron kii mallika lata mangeshkar rafee sahab ke bare kahati hai, 'saral man ke insanrafi sahab bahut sureele the
 It is my luck that i sang the most songs with him
 gaanaa kaisaa bhi ho wo aise ga lete the ki gaanaa naa samajhane vaale bhi vaah-vaah kar uthte the 
 Such singers are not born again and again
 mashhoor geetkaar naushaad ne mohammad rafee ke nidhan par likhaa tha, 'goonjati he teri aawaaj amiron ke mahal main, jhopadon ke garibon main bhi he tere saaj, yun to apane mausiki par sahab ko fakr hota he magar e mere saathi mausiki ko bhi aaj tujh par he naaj'
 3
 mohammad rafee kaa aakhri geet film 'aas paas' ke liye tha, jo unhone lakshmikant pyarelal ke liye apane nidhan se thik do din pehle record kiya tha, geet ke bol the 'shaam phir kyon udhaas he dost'
 4
 mohammad rafee ne kishor kumaar kii filmonke liye bhi geet gaaye hai jinamein film 'bade sarkaar', 'raagini' or kai filmein shaamil thim
 Rafi sang about 11 songs for Kishore Kumar
 5
 While singing the song 'babul Ki Duaan Leet Jaa' from the film 'neel Kamal', Rafi's eyes used to tear repeatedly and the reason behind this was that his daughter got engaged just a day before singing this song
 He was very emotional, yet he sang this song and got the 'national Award' for this song
 6
 In the early days of Hindi cinema, only Mukesh ji and Talatmehmood used to be named, no one knew Rafi but when Naushad gave Rafi a chance for the film 'baiju Bawra', he said that 'with this film , You will dominate everyone's tongue
 And that's what happened
 7
 In 1976, when the film 'laila Majnu' was being made, Rishi Kapoor wanted only Kishore Kumar to sing for him, while composer Madan Mohan said that Mohammad Rafi will sing only in this film, otherwise we will not do the film
 aakhirkaar mohammad rafee ne hi geet gaae or wo itane saraahe gaye kii phir filmon rishi kapur kii aawaaj rafee sahab hi ban gaye
 8
 jis dinamohammad rafee nidhan hua us din mumbaimein joro kii barish ho rahi thi or phir bhi antim yatra ke liye kam se kam 1 xxrep 4 0 log sadakon par the or us din mashhoor actor manoj kumaar ne kaha, 'suron kii maa saraswati bhi apane aansu baha rahi hai aaj'
 9
 rafee ko ghanton geet gane ke baad apni chat par patang udaane kaa bada shauk tha or jab unki patang kabhi cat jaati thi to chote bachche ki tarah machal jate the
 10
 6 filmphere or 1 neshnal award rafee ke naam hai

 International First Aid Day is observed every year on the second Saturday of September
 first aid de ke prati logon ko jaagruk karne ke liye duniyabar main kaaryakramon kaa aayojan kiya jaataa he
 Its purpose is to inform people how to deal with incidents, accidents and emergencies
 first aid kii basic jaankaree bacchon ko dena bahut jaruri he
 In England schools are ready to start the course with first aid soon
 aap bhi apane bacchon ko first aid se judi ye jaankaree de sakate hai
 1
 saans na aane kii sthiti memgar koi aapke saamne achet avasthaa main padaa ho or baar-baar bulaane yaa haath hilaane par bhi jawaab na de to use turant jameen par peeth ke bal leta den
 Check if he is breathing
 sir peeche kar seene par dabaav daalkar teji se ragaden
 If the person still does not get breath, then please give information about calling emergency number
 2
 If you are breathing, but there is no response, if someone is breathing but if they still do not react, then first make them sit comfortably
 phir sir peeche kii taraf kar den
 This will make them easier to breathe
 3
 Try to stop the bleeding from the place where there is excess bleeding
 kisi kapade ko chot kii jagah lagaakar use dabaaen or khun rokane kii koshish karen
 Try to apply some cool thing on their wounds
 isse khun band ho jayega
 4
 sir par chot lagi ho tosir par chot laganaa jaanaleva bhi ho saktaa he
 In case of head injury, apply cold thing on the injury
 aap chahen to tauliye main thandi hari patteydaar subjiyan baandhakar use chot kii jagah laga sakate hai
 This will reduce swelling
 5
 Sometimes there is a complaint of suffocation due to persistent knee or neck stiffness
 aise main saans lene yaa khansane main dikkat hoti he
 In this case, rub the patient's back and pat it slightly
 isse unhen saans lene main thodi aasaani hogi
 In December 1992, after the demolition of Babri Masjid, around 2,000 people were killed
 hajaaron dakshin panthi kaaryakartaaon ne masjid ko dhaha diya tha
 This was done to build a temple at the birthplace of Lord Rama

 dino ne apane kambek ke bare main bataaya, mujhe acchhee script kaa intjaar tha

 aamtaur par chumban kaa prayog kamkrida se pehle kiya jaataa he

 mana gaya he ki sabhi logon ke liye chumban ke taur-tareekon kaa prayog ek jaisaa nahin ho saktaa he

 vah koi cheshtaa nahin karti

 jab stri purush ke hoth ko apane donon hothon main lekar neeche vaale hoth ko fadakaati he, to ise 'sphutaritak' kehete hai
 When the woman presses the lips of the man with her lips and closes the eyes of the man with his hand, and rubs the lips of the man with the tip of his tongue, it is called 'ghatitak' 
 kaamshaastra ke anya vidwaanon ne iske atirikt chaar anya prakaar ke chumban kii charchaa kii he
 When men or women take the lips of another and take it in front of each other, it is called 'sama'
 jab purush yaa stri tirchhe hokar apane hothon ko golakaar dete hue chumban dete hai, to ise 'tiryak' kehete hai

 pehle bataae gaye in teenon prakaar ke chumban ko yadi is prakaar kiya jaae ki duusare ko pidaa ho, to ise 'peditak' kehete hai

 'shuddh peditak' chumban vah he, jinamein keval hothon kaa prayog kiya jaataa he

 chumban kaa ek paanchvaan prakaar bhi he, jise 'avapidit' kaha jaataa he

 ab tak neeche ke hoth ke chumban kaa vivaran diya gaya he

 donon hothon ko apane donon hothon ke bich main dabaakar daanton se peedit karte hue chumnaa 'samputak' chumban kehalaata he

 antat: samprag ke sabase bade ghatak dal congress ne agle varsh hone vaale aam chunaav se pehle sarvasammati se is mudde ko sulajhane ke liye mangalvaar ko baithak bulaai, jisamen pruthak telugana rajya ke gathan ko sarvasammati se sweekruti de di gai
 Several leaders from Seemandhra and Telangana reached Delhi on Tuesday to participate in the upa's coordination committee
 simandhra se kendriya mantriyon sahit kai saansad evam rajya ke anek mantri rajya ke vibhaajan ko rokane ke uddeshy se dilli aae the
 Telangana leaders expressed confidence after a separate meeting that the Congress would realize the long-cherished dream of the people of the region

 who came on the call of the central leadership
 kiran kumaar reddy, up mukhyamantri damodar rajanrasimha or congress ke pradeshdhyaksh botsa satyanarayana aanan-fanan main dilli pahunche tathaa party ke mahasachiv evam pradesh prabharee digvijay singh evam anya kendriya netaaon se mulaakaat kii
 The comments duusari taraf, jammu evam kashmir ke mukhyamantri tathaa samprag ke ghatak dal, neshnal conference ke netaa umr abdulla ne mangalvaar ko kaha ki andolan ke aadhaar par nae rajya ke gathan se 'khatarnaak paripati' banegi
 Abdullah said this would encourage nuisances in other parts of the country
 andhra pradesh ke hi kuch congress saansad bhi pruthak telugana rajya ke gathan kaa virodh kar rahe hai, or is sambandh main pichley saptaah unhone pradhanmantri se bhi mulaakaat kii thi or rajya ko vibhajit na karne kii maang kii thi
 After the meeting held at the Prime Minister's residence on Tuesday, Civil Aviation Minister Ajit Singh said, "all parties have unanimously decided in favor of Telangana
 " Leaders of Congress, Nationalist Congress Party (NCP), National Conference and Rashtriya Lok Dal (RLD) participated in the meeting
 samprag kii samanvay samiti kii baithak ke baad congress kaary samiti (seedblusi) ne bhi ek prastaav paarit kar centre sarkaar se andhra pradesh ko vibhajit kar pruthak telugana rajya ke gathan kaa anurodh kiya
 In the proposal seeking the creation of a separate Telangana, the CWC has said that Hyderabad should be allowed to be the joint capital of Andhra Pradesh and Telangana for the next 10 years
 seedblusi kii baithak ke baad congress ke pravaktaa ajay maakan ne kaha ki seedblusi kii baithak kii adhyakshata party kaa adhyaksh sonia gandhi ne kii tathaa baithak main pradhanmantri manmohan singh or congress ke upaadhyaksh rahul gandhi ne bhi hissaa liya
 Maken read the resolution passed, "it is proposed to request the Central Government to take steps for the formation of a separate Telangana state
" " Union HRD Minister M
 em
 Pallam Raju had earlier indicated that Congress leaders were in favor of deciding to form a separate Telangana state
 andhra state or telugana (tab kaa hyderabad state) ko milakar ek november 1956 ko gathit kiye gaye rajya andhra pradesh ke gathan ke baad se hi chale aa rahe is mudde kaa samprag ke is nirnay ke saath hi patakshep ho gaya
 Andhra Pradesh, formed on a linguistic basis, will be the first state in the country to be partitioned
 rajya banane ke baad telugana kaa kshetrafal 1
 It will be 14 lakh square kilometers and its population will be 35
 38 karod hogi
 Of the 294 assembly seats in Andhra Pradesh, 117 assembly seats are in Telangana, and there are 17 mps in the Lok Sabha from the Telangana region
 telugana ko alag rajya banane ke liye 'jai telugana' andolan main 1969 main 300 se adhik logon kii police golibari main maut ho gai thi, jisamen adhiktar yuva chaatr shaamil the
 The central government started active efforts to form a separate Telangana from 2009 and during this time the Congress, the largest party in the ruling UPA government, suffered a lot in the state elections due to not reaching any concrete decision
 rajya main congress ke anek saansad telugana ke liye sangharsh kar rahi party telugana raashtra samiti (tiares) main shaamil ho gaye
 The TRS and other parties continued to pressurize the central government to constitute a separate Telangana state

 pruthak telugana ke gathan ke liye centre sarkaar ne 2009 se sakriy prayaas shuru kiye or is dauraan kisi thos nirnay par na pahunch paane ke kaaran sattarudh samprag sarkaar kii sabase badi party congress ko rajya ke chunaav main kaaphi nuksaan uthaanaa padaa

 keshav raav ke is mudde par congress se istipha dene ke saath hi congress par is par koi thos nirnay lene kaa dabaav or bad gaya
 Finally, the Congress, the largest constituent of the UPA, called a meeting on Tuesday to resolve the issue unanimously before the general elections due next year, in which the formation of a separate Telangana state was unanimously approved
